<div id="review_759332677" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/759332677" />
    <a title="TeriLyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1459307-terilyn"><img alt="TeriLyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396453806p2/1459307.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/759332677?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TeriLyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TeriLyn" href="/user/show/1459307-terilyn">TeriLyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1459307-terilyn?shelf=2014-favorites">2014-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1459307-terilyn?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1459307-terilyn?shelf=new-adult-favorites">new-adult-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer759332677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1015166391544811828">**ARC generously provided by the author in exchange for an honest review**<br/><br/>5+++ Stars! Sweet Rome is awesome. I absolutely loved Sweet Home, the first book in this series. Sweet Rome is a re-telling of Romeo and Molly's story but from Rome's perspective. It was awesome! Wait, did I already say that? Just reiterating how much I loved it. Seeing this story play out again from Romeo's perspective is like reading an entirely new story. The author's seamless writing takes us inside the beautifully com</span>
  <span id="freeText1015166391544811828" style="display:none">**ARC generously provided by the author in exchange for an honest review**<br /><br />5+++ Stars! Sweet Rome is awesome. I absolutely loved Sweet Home, the first book in this series. Sweet Rome is a re-telling of Romeo and Molly's story but from Rome's perspective. It was awesome! Wait, did I already say that? Just reiterating how much I loved it. Seeing this story play out again from Romeo's perspective is like reading an entirely new story. The author's seamless writing takes us inside the beautifully complicated mind of Romeo Prince. Sweet Rome takes a deeper look into his sordid past and completely unravels his present. We gained a surface level understanding of Rome in the first book but this book just blows those already exceeded expectations right out of the water. His need for Molly and his feelings surrounding his life, his future, and how Molly so perfectly fits into that mold run so much deeper than we could have ever known. I loved his reactions to her. It was fascinating to hear Romeo's thoughts. Sweet Rome also furthers the story after where we were left in Sweet Home. And to top it all off, the cherry on top, we get the sweetest, most awesome, completely satisfying epilogue. And since that could never be enough of these two great characters we get a bonus chapter from Molly's POV. Sweet Rome is a brilliant follow up to Sweet Home. There was nothing disappointing about it. I have found before that the re-telling of a story from a different POV can get redundant. Thanks to Ms. Cole's flawlessly executed, beautiful words it didn't even come close to being boring or repetitive. You’ll fall in love with Romeo and Molly's story all over again and feel so happy after reading that epic epilogue. Bravo! Just awesome!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1015166391544811828" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('B0M147zPAHOJppXlUoLawZGXLXUNjQAGzio0zN4FN9Zc2t6R3dRMYfwiPJO0p0p9ZjuOCVuCsaPDuJ+WqaHjcw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RhU4csa48E+tvfhRvy0RqAVo1+wO1LhSbjZ+kUEnziIdjNMAp6O8Xdg5USdZCIEU8sR0kFjbCfdjpNXLNoMahw==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">About Tillie Cole</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1517004382p3/7074846.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">Tillie Cole

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10799020560823352214">Amazon & USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses.</span>
  <span id="freeText10799020560823352214" style="display:none">Amazon &amp; USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses. <br />Being a scary blend of Scottish and English, Tillie embraces both cultures; her English heritage through her love of HP sauce and freshly made Yorkshire Puddings, and her Scottish which is mostly demonstrated by her frighteningly foul-mouthed episodes of pure rage and her much loved dirty jokes.<br /><br />Having been born and raised as a Teesside Smoggie, Tillie, at age nineteen, moved forty miles north to the 'Toon', Newcastle-Upon-Tyne, where she attended Newcastle University and graduated with a Bachelor of Arts honours degree in Religious Studies. She returned two years later to complete a Post-Graduate Certificate in Teaching High School Social Studies. Tillie, regards Newcastle to be a home from home and enjoyed the Newcastle Geordie way of life for seven 'proper mint' and 'lush' years.<br /><br />One summers day, after finishing reading her thousandth book on her much loved and treasured Kindle, Tillie turned to her husband and declared, "D'you know, I have a great idea for a story. I could write a book." Several months later, after repeating the same tired line at the close of another completed story, she was scolded by her husband to shut up talking about writing a novel and "just bloody do it!" For the first time in eleven years, Tillie actually took his advice (he is still trying to get over the shock) and immediately set off on a crazy journey, delving deep into her fertile imagination. <br /><br />Tillie, ever since, has written from the heart. She combines her passion for anything camp and glittery with her love of humour and dark brooding men (most often muscled and tattooed – they’re her weakness!). She also has a serious side (believe it or not!) and loves to immerse herself in the complex study of World Religions, History and Cultural Studies and creates fantasy stories that enable her to thread serious issues and topics into her writing -- yep, there's more to this girl than profanity and sparkles!<br /><br />After six years of teaching high school Social Studies and following her Professional Rugby Player husband around Europe, they have finally given up their nomadic way of life and settled in Calgary, Alberta where Tillie spends most of her days (and many a late night) lost in a writing euphoria or pursuing a dazzling career as a barrel-racing, tasselled-chap wearing, Stetson-sporting cowgirl... Ye-haw!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10799020560823352214" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

I was Ally, the best friend to the most amazing group of girls I\'ve ever known—a title I loved, but one I became tired of \'just\' being. And I was Ally, the one on which they could all rely.\n\nBut to me, I was Ally, the girl with the heart no one had claimed... And I was, Ally, the girl, who underneath it all, was heart-breakingly lonely.\n\nI LOVE love; the thought of it, the nervous excitement of falling for Mr. Right, the desire of someone becoming my entire world... of me becoming theirs. I’ve always wanted passion, heart-stopping, epic, life-changing romance... I’ve always wanted the fairytale… I’ve always wanted it all.\n\nIt just never seemed like I would get it.\n\nFor the past few years I\'ve thrown myself into my career as a museum curator. I’m the best of the best, the person every museum wants to hire, so when an opportunity came up to move to Seattle, I jumped at the chance. My cousin and my best friend lived in Seattle and I needed a change. \n\nI needed a new beginning.\n\nI wasn\'t expecting to meet anyone in the Emerald City. I wasn\'t expecting to work closely with the reclusive new sculptor my all-important gallery design was centered around. And I certainly wasn\'t expecting to fall for him... heart-stopping, epic, life-changing love...\nMy real life fairytale come true.\n\nBut, like in every fairytale, there’s a villain, a dark and tortured soul... I just didn\'t know that the villain and the hero in my story would end up being one and the same.\n\nNew Adult Romance Novel—contains adult content, sexual situations and mature topics.
